CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Orders (order_id INT PRIMARY KEY, product_id INT, supplier_id INT, quantity INT, order_date DATE);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS Products (product_id INT PRIMARY KEY, product_name STRING, quantity INT, price DECIMAL);</t><s>REVOKE SELECT, INSERT, UPDATE ON Orders FROM public</s>
